d="M3.81183 6.65363C4.12865 6.33681 4.64232 6.33681 4.95913 6.65363L10.0643 11.7588L15.1696 6.65363C15.4864 6.33681 16 6.33681 16.3169 6.65363C16.6337 6.97045 16.6337 7.48411 16.3169 7.80093L10.6437 13.4741C10.3237 13.7941 9.80493 13.794 9.48496 13.4741L3.81183 7.80093C3.49501 7.48411 3.49501 6.97045 3.81183 6.65363Z" fill="#001435"></path></svg></div><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/reporting/overview"><button class="menu__link" pa-marked="1">Reporting</button></a></div><ul class="menu-list__hidden"><li class="menu__item"><div Cards</button></a></div></li><li class="menu__item"><div class="menu-item__title"><div class="menu-item__dropdown"></div><a class="menu-item__title"><div class="menu-item__dropdown"></div><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/reporting/transaction-level-fee-report"><button class="menu__link" Fields</button></a></div></li></ul></div></div></aside></div></div><div id="contentContainer" class="flex-content"><main id="main-section" class="documentation-content__wrapper"><article class="main-content js-outlet docs--constrained"><div class="subtitle-container"><div class="breadcrumb breadcrumbInner"><div class="breadcrumbItem"><a class="breadcrumbLink">Control Panel</a><span 4px">/</span></div><div class="breadcrumbItem"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines" class="activeBreadcrumbLink">Declines</a></div></div><div class="markdownopts-container"><div class="markdownopts-face-container"><button class="markdownopts-face-button"><svg fill="#000000" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:16px;height:16px;margin-right:8px"><title>OpenAI icon</title><path d="M22.2819 9.8211a5.9847 5.9847 0 0 0-.5157-4.9108 6.0462 6.0462 0 0 .3927-.6813v-6.7369l2.02 1.1686a.071.071 0 0 1 .038.052v5.5826a4.504 4.504 0 0 1-4.4945 4.4944zm-9.6607-4.1254a4.4708 4.4708 0 0 1-.5346-3.0137l.142.0852 4.783 2.7582a.7712.7712 0 0 0 .7806 1.1685a.0757.0757 0 0 1-.071 0l-4.8303-2.7865A4.504 4.504 0 0 1 2.3408 7.872zm16.5963 3.8558L13.1038 8.364 15.1192 7.2a.0757.0757 0 0 1 .071 0l4.8303 2.7913a4.4944 4.4944 0 0 1-.6765 8.1042v-5.6772a.79.79 0 0 0-.407-.667zm2.0107-3.0231l-.142-.0852-4.7735-2.7818a.7759.7759 0 0 0-.7854 0L9.409 9.2297V6.8974a.0662.0662 0 0 1 .0284-.0615l4.8303-2.7866a4.4992 4.4992 0 0 1 6.6802 4.66zM8.3065 12.863l-2.02-1.1638a.0804.0804 0 0 1-.038-.0567V6.0742a4.4992 4.4992 0 0 1 7.3757-3.4537l-.142.0805L8.704 5.459a.7948.7948 0 0 0-.3927.6813zm1.0976-2.3654l2.602-1.4998 2.6069 1.4998v2.9994l-2.5974 1.4997-2.6067-1.4997Z"></path></svg>Ask ChatGPT</button><button class="markdownopts-chevron-button" data-testid="chevron-button"><style data-emotion="css 1bk0n6-svg-size_md">.css-1bk0n6-svg-size_md{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:2rem;height:2rem;}.css-1bk0n6-svg-size_md img,.css-1bk0n6-svg-size_md svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="css-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" style="width:16px;height:16px" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4.292 8.293a1 1 0 0 1 1.414 0L12 14.586l6.293-6.293a1 1 0 0 1 1.414 1.414L12.713 16.7a1.01 1.01 0 0 1-1.428 0L4.292 9.707a1 1 0 0 1 0-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></button></div></div></div><div class="main-article-content"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><section><h1><span>Declines</span></h1><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><p class="markdown-p"><span>
            Declines are not the same as gateway rejections. Declined transactions are blocked by the
            customer's bank, while
            </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/gateway-rejections"><span>gateway rejections</span></a><span>
            are blocked by your Braintree gateway settings.
        </span></p></span></div></div><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        A processor decline indicates that the customer’s bank has refused the transaction request.
        Sometimes you can tell why it was declined by reading the response code, but only the customer's
        bank can confirm the specific reason.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>The most common reasons for declines are:</span></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>Incorrect credit card number or expiration date</span></li><li><span>Insufficient funds</span></li><li><span>The bank declined based on location</span></li><li><span>The bank's fraud rules blocked the transaction</span></li></ul><h2 id="decline-ratios" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Decline ratios</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#decline-ratios" aria-label="Decline ratios"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        An acceptable decline ratio is about 10% of your transactions, but this may fluctuate based on
        industry or business model. You can analyze your decline ratio by
        </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/reporting/decline-analysis"><span>creating a decline report</span></a><span>.
    </span></p><h3 id="lowering-your-decline-ratio" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Lowering your decline ratio</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#lowering-your-decline-ratio" aria-label="Lowering your decline ratio"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        While declines are usually influenced by the customer's bank, your decline ratio can be inflated
        by repeated attempts on the same payment method – either on your end or by the customer.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        We recommend that you use our
        </span><a href="/braintree/articles/guides/fraud-tools/basic/risk-threshold-rules"><span>risk threshold rules</span></a><span>
        to reduce repeated customer attempts and our
        </span><a href="/braintree/articles/guides/recurring-billing/recurring-advanced-settings#automatic-retries"><span>automated retry logic for subscriptions</span></a><span>
        instead of implementing your own.
    </span></p><h2 id="authorization-declines" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Authorization declines</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#authorization-declines" aria-label="Authorization declines"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        When we talk about declines, we're usually referring to authorization declines. These happen when
        you request authorization to charge a customer's payment method, and the bank refuses to authorize
        the charge.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#authorization-decline-codes"><span>See the complete list of authorization decline codes.</span></a></p><h2 id="settlement-declines" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Settlement declines</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#settlement-declines" aria-label="Settlement declines"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        Settlement declines happen when the bank denies the transaction after a successful authorization.
        These are much more rare than authorization declines.
        </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#settlement-declined"><span>Learn more about settlement declined transactions in our developer docs.</span></a></p><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#settlement-decline-codes"><span>See the complete list of settlement decline codes.</span></a></p><h2 id="handling-declines" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Handling declines</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#handling-declines" aria-label="Handling declines"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        There are two types of declines: hard and soft declines. The type of decline informs how you
        should handle it.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><strong><span>Hard declines</span></strong><span> are the result of an error or issue which can't be resolved
        immediately. Action such as contacting Braintree Support or asking the customer to contact their
        bank will need to be taken to resolve the issue before the transaction can be retried.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><strong><span>Soft declines</span></strong><span> are the result of a temporary issue. Retrying the provided payment
        method information may be successful.
    </span></p><h2 id="retrying-declined-transactions" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Retrying declined transactions</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#retrying-declined-transactions" aria-label="Retrying declined transactions"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        Recently, Visa and MasterCard have implemented new fees to maintain network health by curbing
        excessive retries across each decline code category. These recent mandates affect every Payment
        Service Provider (PSP), including Braintree.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        Transactions that are being fined are merchant-initiated or customer-initiated retries, or new
        transaction attempts from customers that are being flagged as retries.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        If you decide to manage your retries internally, note how retries are identifiable from
        Braintree's response codes.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        Retries for both Visa and Mastercard can have fees associated with them based on the number of
        re-attempts made.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Visa</span></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>For Visa, retry categories are mapped to Braintree response codes as follows:</span></p><style data-emotion="css 19859z6-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">.css-19859z6-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100{color:#202020;font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,"Helvetica Code</span></th><th><span>Retry Guidance</span></th><th><span>Fee</span></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><span>Category 1</span></td><td><a                     </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2007"><span>2007</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2009"><span>2009</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2108"><span>2108</span></a><span>,

                    $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international
                    transaction beyond threshold.
                </span></td></tr><tr><td><span>Category 2</span></td><td><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2026"><span>2026</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2038"><span>2038</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2001"><span>2001</span></a><span>,
                    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2014"><span>2014</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2002"><span>2002</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2057"><span>2057</span></a><span>,
                    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2003"><span>2003</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2101"><span>2101</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2107"><span>2107</span></a><span>,
                    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2038"><span>2038*</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2046"><span>2046</span></a><span>,
                    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2020"><span>2020</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-3000"><span>3000</span></a></td><td><span>
                    Issuer Cannot Approve At this Time (Reattempt Allowed); limit retries to 15 retries over a
                    rolling 30 day period
                </span></td><td><span>
                    $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international
                    transaction beyond threshold.
                </span></td></tr><tr><td><span>Category 3</span></td><td><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2004"><span>2004</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2007"><span>2007</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2102"><span>2102</span></a><span>,
                    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2010"><span>2010</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2101"><span>2101</span></a><span>, </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2103"><span>2103</span></a><span>,
                    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2038"><span>2038* </span></a></td><td><span>Limit retries to 15 retries over a rolling 30 day period</span></td><td><span>
                    $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international
                    transaction beyond threshold.
                </span></td></tr><tr><td><span>Category 4</span></td><td><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2000"><span>2000</span></a></td><td><span>Limit retries to 15 retries over a rolling 30 day period</span></td><td><span>
                    $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international
                    transaction beyond threshold.
                </span></td></tr></tbody></table><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>
            Braintree Response code 2038 is mapped to Visa network response codes categorized as Category 2
            and Category 3. In either situation, the recommendation is to limit retries to 15 over 30 days.
        </span></li></ul><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><p class="markdown-p"><strong><u><span>Note:</span></u></strong><span> Retrying Category 1 declines carry the highest network fees
            because each retry attempt is fined. Contact your CSM or reach out to support to stop Braintree
            retries, including retrying Category 1 declines. Stopping retries, including Category 1
            declines, may impact your recovery rate.
        </span></p></span></div></div><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Mastercard</span></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        For Mastercard, retries should be based only on the Merchant Advice Codes found in the
        merchant_advice_code field and its corresponding description merchant_advice_code_text. Mastercard
        assesses a $0.10 fee for every reattempt exceeding 10 retries over a 24-hour period for MAC 03 and
        MAC 21.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        For the specific rules around retries for Mastercard,see the
        </span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/docs/reference/general/merchant-responses/merchant-advice-codes"><span>Braintree Merchant Advice Codes</span></a><span>
        page.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Braintree Smart Retries</span></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Merchants can retry transactions using:</span></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>Braintree Retry, which uses static logic to reattempt a transaction.</span></li><li><span>
            Smart Retries, a machine-learning-based solution to help optimize retry strategies and increase
            the success rate of a transaction.
        </span></li></ul><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        Smart Retries help predict better retry strategies from inputs based on varying factors, from
        customer behavior, transaction history, and payment processing performance. Smart Retries can also
        help minimize payment friction at checkout by potentially reducing transaction latency, helping to
        drive revenue and customer satisfaction.
    </span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Merchants currently using Braintree Retry will be migrated to Smart Retries.</span></p><h2 id="additional-processor-responses" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Additional Processor Responses</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#additional-processor-responses" aria-label="Additional Processor Responses"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        As a supplement to processor response codes, you can choose to enable additional processor
        responses in the Control Panel. If enabled – and the processor declines the transaction – the
        processor’s raw response will be displayed in the transaction details in the Control Panel. This
        response doesn’t often offer much additional context, which is why this feature is disabled by
        default. If you would like to enable it:
    </span></p><ol class="list list--num"><li><span>Log into the </span><a href="https://www.braintreegateway.com/login"><span>Control Panel</span></a></li><li><span>Click on the gear icon in the top right corner</span></li><li><span>Click </span><strong><span>Processing</span></strong><span> from the drop-down menu</span></li><li><span>Scroll to the </span><strong><span>Transactions</span></strong><span> section</span></li><li><span>
            Next to </span><strong><span>Display Additional Processor Response</span></strong><span>, click the toggle to turn it on
        </span></li></ol><p class="markdown-p"><span>
        Regardless of whether you enable this feature in the Control Panel, the API will always return the
        additional processor response in the
        </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction#processor-declined"><span>transaction object</span></a><span>.
    </span></p><h2 id="authorization-decline-codes" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Authorization decline codes</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#authorization-decline-codes" aria-label="Authorization decline codes"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><style data-emotion="css                             information. Have the customer correct their payment information and attempt the

                            the customer will need to contact their bank.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 3, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2011" id="code-2011" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2011"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2011</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Voice Authorization Required</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer’s bank is requesting that the merchant (you) call to obtain a special
                            authorization code in order to complete this transaction. This can result in a lengthy
                            process – we recommend obtaining a new payment method instead.</span></em></p><em></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Contact us</span></em></p></a><em></em><p class="markdown-p"><span>for more details.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2012" id="code-2012" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2012"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2012</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Processor Declined – Possible Lost Card</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The card used has likely been reported as lost. The customer will need to contact their
                            bank for more information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2013" id="code-2013" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2013"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2013</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Processor Declined – Possible Stolen Card</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The card used has likely been reported as stolen. The customer will need to contact
                            their bank for more information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2014" id="code-2014" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2014"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2014</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Processor Declined – Fraud Suspected</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer’s bank suspects fraud – they will need to contact their bank for more
                            information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2015" id="code-2015" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2015"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2015</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Transaction Not Allowed</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer's bank is declining the transaction for unspecified reasons, possibly due
                            to an issue with the card itself. They will need to contact their bank or use a
                            different payment method.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 1, do not retry</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2016" id="code-2016" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2016"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2016</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Duplicate Transaction</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The submitted transaction appears to be a duplicate of a previously submitted
                            transaction and was declined to prevent charging the same card twice for the same
                            service.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2017" id="code-2017" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2017"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2017</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Cardholder Stopped Billing</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer requested a cancellation of a single transaction – reach out to them for
                            more information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 1, do not retry</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2018" id="code-2018" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2018"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2018</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Cardholder Stopped All Billing</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer requested the cancellation of a recurring transaction or subscription –
                            reach out to them for more information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 1, do not retry</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2019" id="code-2019" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2019"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2019</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Invalid Transaction</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer’s bank declined the transaction, typically because the card in question
                            does not support this type of transaction – for example, the customer used an FSA debit
                            card for a non-healthcare related purchase. They will need to contact their bank for
                            more information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 1, do not retry</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2020" id="code-2020" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2020"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2020</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Violation</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer will need to contact their bank for more information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2021" id="code-2021" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2021"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2021</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Security Violation</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer's bank is declining the transaction, possibly due to a fraud concern. They
                            will need to contact their bank or use a different payment method.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2022" id="code-2022" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2022"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2022</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Declined – Updated Cardholder Available</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The submitted card has expired or been reported lost and a new card has been issued.
                            Reach out to your customer to obtain updated card information.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2023" id="code-2023" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2023"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2023</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Processor Does Not Support This Feature</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Your account can't process transactions with the intended feature – for example, 3D
                            Secure or Level 2/Level 3 data. If you believe your merchant account should be set up to
                            accept this type of transaction,</span></em></p><em></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>contact us</span></em></p></a><em></em><p class="markdown-p"><span>.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2024" id="code-2024" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2024"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2024</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Card Type Not Enabled</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Your account can't process the attempted card type. If you believe your merchant
                            account should be set up to accept this type of card,</span></em></p><em></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>contact us</span></em></p></a><em></em><p class="markdown-p"><span>for assistance.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2025" id="code-2025" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2025"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2025</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Set Up Error – Merchant</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Depending on your region, this response could indicate a connectivity or setup
                            issue.</span></em></p><em></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Contact us</span></em></p></a><em></em><p class="markdown-p"><span>for more information regarding this error message.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2026" id="code-2026" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2026"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2026</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Invalid Merchant ID</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer’s bank declined the transaction, typically because the card in question
                            does not support this type of transaction. If this response persists across transactions
                            for multiple customers, it could indicate a connectivity or setup issue.</span></em></p><em></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Contact us</span></em></p></a><em></em><p class="markdown-p"><span>for more information regarding this error message.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2027" id="code-2027" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2027"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2027</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Set Up Error – Amount</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>This rare decline code indicates an issue with processing the amount of the
                            transaction. The customer will need to contact their bank for more details.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2028" id="code-2028" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2028"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2028</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Set Up Error – Hierarchy</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>There is a setup issue with your account.</span></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><em><span>Contact us</span></em></a><em><span>for more information.</span></em></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2029" id="code-2029" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2029"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2029</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Set Up Error – Card</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>This response generally indicates that there is a problem with the submitted card.                             customer will need to use a different payment method.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2030" id="code-2030" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2030"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2030</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Set Up Error – Terminal</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>There is a setup issue with your account.</span></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><em><span>Contact us</span></em></a><em><span>for more information.</span></em></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2031" id="code-2031" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2031"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2031</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Encryption Error</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The cardholder’s bank does not support $0.00 card verifications.                             payment method.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2033" id="code-2033" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2033"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2033</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Inconsistent Data</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>An error occurred when communicating with the processor.                             the customer attempt the transaction again – if the decline persists, the customer will
                            need to use a different payment method.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2036" id="code-2036" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2036"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2036</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Authorization could not be found</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>An error occurred when trying to process the authorization. Have the customer attempt
                            the transaction again – if the decline persists,</span></em></p><em></em><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction"><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>contact us</span></em></p></a><em></em><p class="markdown-p"><span>for more information.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2041" id="code-2041" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2041"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2041</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Declined – Call For Approval</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The card used for this transaction requires customer approval – they will need to

Pick Up Card</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The customer’s card has been reported as lost or stolen by the cardholder and the

Please try a different US bank account verification method.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2093" id="code-2093" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2093"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2093</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal payment method is invalid</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>The PayPal payment method has either expired or been canceled.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2094" id="code-2094" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2094"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2094</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal payment has already been completed</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Your integration is likely making PayPal calls out of sequence.                             response for more details.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Hard</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-2095" id="code-2095" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-2095"><p class="markdown-p"><span>2095</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal refund is not allowed after partial refund</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>Once a PayPal transaction is partially refunded, all subsequent refunds must also be

                            contact their bank for more details regarding this generic decline.</span></em></p><em></em><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Soft</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"></td></tr><tr data-hashlink="#code-3000" id="code-3000" class="selectable-row"><td width="125" valign="top"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-3000"><p class="markdown-p"><span>3000</span></p></a></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Processor Network Unavailable – Try Again</span></p><p class="markdown-p"></p></td><td width="125" valign="top"><p class="markdown-p"><em></em></p><p class="markdown-p"><em><span>This response could indicate a problem with the back-end processing network, not

class="table--selectable-row ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ecmTable articlesTable css-19859z6-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100"><thead><tr id="code-header"><th><p class="markdown-p"><span>Code</span></p></th><th><p class="markdown-p"><span>Text</span></p></th><th><p class="markdown-p"><span>Explanation</span></p></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="code-4001" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4001"><span>4001</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Settlement Declined</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>The processor declined to settle the sale or refund request.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4003" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4003"><span>4003</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Already Captured</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>The transaction has already been fully captured.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4004" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4004"><span>4004</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Already Refunded</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>The transaction has already been fully refunded.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4005" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4005"><span>4005</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Risk Rejected</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>The sale request was rejected by PayPal risk.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4006" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4006"><span>4006</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Capture Amount Exceeded Allowable Limit</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>The specified capture amount exceeded the amount allowed by the processor.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4018" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4018"><span>4018</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Pending Payments Not Supported</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>
                        PayPal returned a pending sale or refund response which is disallowed by Braintree. This
                        failure is likely due to a misconfiguration in your PayPal account. Further details may be
                        found in the transaction details.
                    </span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4019" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4019"><span>4019</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Refund Transaction with an Open Case Not Allowed</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>
                        PayPal declined to settle the refund request as there is an open dispute against the
                        transaction. If you have enabled PayPal disputes within Braintree, you may resolve the
                        dispute within the Braintree disputes dashboard. Otherwise, you may do so via your PayPal
                        account's Resolution Center.
                    </span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4020" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4020"><span>4020</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Refund Attempt Limit Reached</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal's maximum number of refund attempts for this transaction has been exceeded.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4021" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4021"><span>4021</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Refund Transaction Not Allowed</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal does not allow you to refund this type of transaction.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4022" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4022"><span>4022</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Refund Invalid Partial Amount</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>The partial refund amount is not valid.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4023" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4023"><span>4023</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal Refund Merchant Account Missing ACH</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Your PayPal account does not have an associated verified bank account.</span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4024" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4024"><span>4024</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Refund Time Limit Exceeded</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>
                        PayPal requires that refunds are issued within 180 days of the sale. This refund can't be
                        successfully processed.
                    </span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4025" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4025"><span>4025</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>Payer Account Is Locked Or Closed</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>
                        The customer’s PayPal account can't be used for transactions at this time. The customer
                        will need to
                        </span><a href="/braintree/articles/guides/payment-methods/paypal/setup-guide#contacting-paypal-support" pa-marked="1"><span>contact PayPal's Support team</span></a><span>
                        for more information or use a different payment method.
                    </span></p></td></tr><tr id="code-4026" class="selectable-row"><td><p class="markdown-p"><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/declines#code-4026"><span>4026</span></a></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>PayPal or Venmo account not configured to refund more than settled amount</span></p></td><td><p class="markdown-p"><span>
                        Your PayPal or Venmo account is not set up to refund amounts higher than the original
                        transaction amount.
                        </span><a href="/braintree/articles/guides/payment-methods/paypal/setup-guide#contacting-paypal-support" pa-marked="1"><span>Contact PayPal's Support team</span></a><span>
                        for information on how to enable this for your PayPal account.
                    </span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></section></div><nav class="right-nav-container"><h4 class="right-nav-title">On this page</h4><ul queryParamters = { eventSource, isQueryEncoded: true, page: '', component: '', eventSourceUrl: '', expireCookies: true }; if (window) { queryParamters.page = window.fpti && window.fpti.page || window.location && window.location.href; queryParamters.component = window.fpti && window.fpti.comp; const eventSourceUrl = window.location && window.location.href; queryParamters.eventSourceUrl = eventSourceUrl && eventSourceUrl.split("?")[0]; } const xhr = window.XMLHttpRequest ? new XMLHttpRequest() : new ActiveXObject('Microsoft.XMLHTTP'); let queryString = ''; Object.keys(queryParamters).forEach((key, index) => queryString += (index > 0 ? true; xhr.onreadystatechange = function () { if (xhr.readyState > 3 && xhr.status === 200) { try { if (xhr?.response && xhr.response != "OK") { const invalidCookies = JSON.parse(xhr?.response)?.invalidCookies; if (invalidCookies.length > 0) { const hostName = document.location.hostname; let subDomains = [hostName]; const parts = hostName.split('.'); parts.forEach((e, i) => {  if(e !== "www"){ subDomains.push("." + parts.slice(i).join('.')); } }); subDomains.pop(); invalidCookies.forEach(cookie => { document.cookie = cookie + '=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=.paypal.com'; document.cookie = cookie + '=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;'; subDomains.forEach(domain => { document.cookie = cookie + '=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=' + domain; }) }) } } } catch (error) { } } }; xhr.setRequestHeader('Accept', 'application/json'); xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json'); xhr.send(); }; function cookieFiltering(eventSource="cookieBanner"){ if(!true || false){ return; } cookieFilteringRequest(eventSource); } function postAjax(isFptiDataAvailable , cookieObj ) { if(!isFptiDataAvailable && getFptiReqData()){  isFptiDataAvailable = true; } if(isFptiDataAvailable){ acceptDeclineFptiEvents(cookieObj); } var xhr = window.XMLHttpRequest ? new 'application/json'); xhr.send(null); return xhr; }; function fptiRecordClick(bannerData){ window.PAYPAL.analytics.Analytics.prototype.recordClick({ data: {...bannerData, product:"cookieBanner"}}); }; cookiesText, c_prefs: cookiePrefs, opsel: cookiePrefs + ',US', csource: 'cookie', event_name: eventName }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ bannerData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; acEventName }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ updatedFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; for(var key in updatedFptiData){ winFptiData[key] = updatedFptiData[key]; }; fptiLogActivity(winFptiData); }; function cookieObjSetup (type) { const cookieObjValue = { "accept" : { endPointSuffix : '&type=explicit_banner&country=US&policy=ccpa&version=v14', endPointPrefix : 'T=1,P=1,F=1,type=explicit_close', eventName : 'cookie_banner_close_clicked', acEventName : 'cookie_banner_closed' } }; return cookieObjValue[type]; } function bindGdprEvents () { var acceptAllButton "}]},{"node":"text","text":"\n"}]}]}},"links":[{"rel":"self","method":"GET","href":"https://api.paypal.com/v2/content/environments/8d3ea1d0-5ecc-4d06-98d9-3c97e7739437/entries/dZ8aJD7gFD7dElGI6jlD7Z"}],"ecm":{"envAllowsPreview":true},"markdown":"---\ntitle: Declines\nslug: /articles/control-panel/transactions/declines/\ncreateTime: '2025-04-01T22:01:18.897Z'\nupdateTime: '2025-04-01T22:01:19.015Z'\n---\n\n\n\n# Declines\n\n\n**NOTE**\n Declines are not the same as gateway rejections. Declined transactions are blocked by the customer's bank, while [gateway rejections](/braintree/articles/control-panel/transactions/gateway-rejections) are blocked by your Braintree gateway settings.\n\n \n\nA processor decline indicates that the customer’s bank has refused the transaction request. Sometimes you can tell why it was declined by reading the response code, but only the customer's bank can confirm the specific reason.\n\nThe most common reasons for declines are:\n\n\n- Incorrect credit card number or expiration date\n- Insufficient funds\n- The bank declined based on location\n- The bank's fraud rules blocked the transaction\n\n\n## Decline ratios\n\nAn acceptable decline ratio is about 10% of your transactions, but this may fluctuate based on industry or business model. You can analyze your decline ratio by [creating a decline report](/braintree/articles/control-panel/reporting/decline-analysis).\n\n\n### Lowering your decline ratio\n\nWhile declines are usually influenced by the customer's bank, your decline ratio can be inflated by repeated attempts on the same payment method – either on your end or by the customer.\n\nWe recommend that you use our [risk threshold rules](/braintree/articles/guides/fraud-tools/basic/risk-threshold-rules) to reduce repeated customer attempts and our [automated retry logic for subscriptions](/braintree/articles/guides/recurring-billing/recurring-advanced-settings#automatic-retries) instead of implementing your own.\n\n\n## Authorization declines\n\nWhen we talk about declines, we're usually referring to authorization declines. These happen when you request authorization to charge a customer's payment method, and the bank refuses to authorize the charge.\n\n[See the complete list of authorization decline codes.](#authorization-decline-codes)\n\n\n## Settlement declines\n\nSettlement declines happen when the bank denies the transaction after a successful authorization. These are much more rare than authorization declines. [Learn more about settlement declined transactions in our developer docs.](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#settlement-declined)\n\n[See the complete list of settlement decline codes.](#settlement-decline-codes)\n\n\n## Handling declines\n\nThere are two types of declines: hard and soft declines. The type of decline informs how you should handle it.\n\n**Hard declines** are the result of an error or issue which can't be resolved immediately. Action such as contacting Braintree Support or asking the customer to contact their bank will need to be taken to resolve the issue before the transaction can be retried.\n\n**Soft declines** are the result of a temporary issue. Retrying the provided payment method information may be successful.\n\n\n## Retrying declined transactions\n\nRecently, Visa and MasterCard have implemented new fees to maintain network health by curbing excessive retries across each decline code category. These recent mandates affect every Payment Service Provider (PSP), including Braintree.\n\nTransactions that are being fined are merchant-initiated or customer-initiated retries, or new transaction attempts from customers that are being flagged as retries.\n\nIf you decide to manage your retries internally, note how retries are identifiable from Braintree's response codes.\n\nRetries for both Visa and Mastercard can have fees associated with them based on the number of re-attempts made.\n\nVisa\n\nFor Visa, retry categories are mapped to Braintree response codes as follows:\n\n| Visa Retry Category | Braintree Response Code | Retry Guidance | Fee |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| Category 1 | [2044](#code-2044),[2047](#code-2047),[2019](#code-2019),[2007](#code-2007),[2009](#code-2009),[2108](#code-2108),[2015](#code-2015),[2017](#code-2017),[2018](#code-2018) | Do not retry | $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international transaction beyond threshold. |\n| Category 2 | [2026](#code-2026),[2038](#code-2038),[2001](#code-2001),[2014](#code-2014),[2002](#code-2002),[2057](#code-2057),[2003](#code-2003),[2101](#code-2101),[2107](#code-2107),[2038*](#code-2038),[2046](#code-2046),[2020](#code-2020),[3000](#code-3000) | Issuer Cannot Approve At this Time (Reattempt Allowed); limit retries to 15 retries over a rolling 30 day period | $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international transaction beyond threshold. |\n| Category 3 | [2004](#code-2004),[2007](#code-2007),[2102](#code-2102),[2010](#code-2010),[2101](#code-2101),[2103](#code-2103),[2038*](#code-2038) | Limit retries to 15 retries over a rolling 30 day period | $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international transaction beyond threshold. |\n| Category 4 | [2000](#code-2000) | Limit retries to 15 retries over a rolling 30 day period | $0.10 for each domestic transaction beyond threshold. $0.15 for each international transaction beyond threshold. |\n\n\n- Braintree Response code 2038 is mapped to Visa network response codes categorized as Category 2 and Category 3. In either situation, the recommendation is to limit retries to 15 over 30 days.\n\n\n**NOTE**\n **Note:** Retrying Category 1 declines carry the highest network fees because each retry attempt is fined. Contact your CSM or reach out to support to stop Braintree retries, including retrying Category 1 declines. Stopping retries, including Category 1 declines, may impact your recovery rate.\n\n \n\nMastercard\n\nFor Mastercard, retries should be based only on the Merchant Advice Codes found in the merchant_advice_code field and its corresponding description merchant_advice_code_text. Mastercard assesses a $0.10 fee for every reattempt exceeding 10 retries over a 24-hour period for MAC 03 and MAC 21.\n\nFor the specific rules around retries for Mastercard,see the [Braintree Merchant Advice Codes](https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/docs/reference/general/merchant-responses/merchant-advice-codes) page.\n\nBraintree Smart Retries\n\nMerchants can retry transactions using:\n\n\n- Braintree Retry, which uses static logic to reattempt a transaction.\n- Smart Retries, a machine-learning-based solution to help optimize retry strategies and increase the success rate of a transaction.\n\nSmart Retries help predict better retry strategies from inputs based on varying factors, from customer behavior, transaction history, and payment processing performance. Smart Retries can also help minimize payment friction at checkout by potentially reducing transaction latency, helping to drive revenue and customer satisfaction.\n\nMerchants currently using Braintree Retry will be migrated to Smart Retries.\n\n\n## Additional Processor Responses\n\nAs a supplement to processor response codes, you can choose to enable additional processor responses in the Control Panel. If enabled – and the processor declines the transaction – the processor’s raw response will be displayed in the transaction details in the Control Panel. This response doesn’t often offer much additional context, which is why this feature is disabled by default. If you would like to enable it:\n\n\n- Log into the[Control Panel](https://www.braintreegateway.com/login)\n- Click on the gear icon in the top right corner\n- Click**Processing**from the drop-down menu\n- Scroll to the**Transactions**section\n- Next to**Display Additional Processor Response**, click the toggle to turn it on\n\nRegardless of whether you enable this feature in the Control Panel, the API will always return the additional processor response in the [transaction object](/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction#processor-declined).\n\n\n## Authorization decline codes\n\n| **Code** | **Text** | **Implications** | **Type** | **Retry Guidance** |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| [2000\n\n](#code-2000) | Do Not Honor | The customer's bank is unwilling to accept the transaction. The customer will need to contact their bank for more details regarding this generic decline. | Soft | Visa: Category 4, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2001\n\n](#code-2001) | Insufficient Funds | The account did not have sufficient funds to cover the transaction amount at the time of the transaction – subsequent attempts at a later date may be successful. | Soft | Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2002\n\n](#code-2002) | Limit Exceeded | The attempted transaction exceeds the withdrawal limit of the account. The customer will need to contact their bank to change the account limits or use a different payment method. | Soft | Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2003\n\n](#code-2003) | Cardholder's Activity Limit Exceeded | The attempted transaction exceeds the activity limit of the account. The customer will need to contact their bank to change the account limits or use a different payment method. | Soft | Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2004\n\n](#code-2004) | Expired Card | Card is expired. The customer will need to use a different payment method. | Hard | Visa: Category 3, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2005\n\n](#code-2005) | Invalid Credit Card Number | The customer entered an invalid payment method or made a typo in their credit card information. Have the customer correct their payment information and attempt the transaction again – if the decline persists, they will need to contact their bank. | Hard |  |\n| [2006\n\n](#code-2006) | Invalid Expiration Date | The customer entered an invalid payment method or made a typo in their card expiration date. Have the customer correct their payment information and attempt the transaction again – if the decline persists, they will need to contact their bank. | Hard |  |\n| [2007\n\n](#code-2007) | No Account | The submitted card number is not on file with the card-issuing bank. The customer will need to contact their bank. | Hard | Visa: Category 3, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2008\n\n](#code-2008) | Card Account Length Error | The submitted card number does not include the proper number of digits. Have the customer attempt the transaction again – if the decline persists, the customer will need to contact their bank. | Hard |  |\n| [2009\n\n](#code-2009) | No Such Issuer | This decline code could indicate that the submitted card number does not correlate to an existing card-issuing bank or that there is a connectivity error with the issuer. The customer will need to contact their bank for more information. | Hard | Visa: Category 1, do not retry |\n| [2010\n\n](#code-2010) | Card Issuer Declined CVV | The customer entered in an invalid security code or made a typo in their card information. Have the customer attempt the transaction again – if the decline persists, the customer will need to contact their bank. | Hard | Visa: Category 3, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2011\n\n](#code-2011) | Voice Authorization Required | The customer’s bank is requesting that the merchant (you) call to obtain a special authorization code in order to complete this transaction. This can result in a lengthy process – we recommend obtaining a new payment method instead.\n\n[Contact us\n\n](https://developer.paypal.com/braintree/help?issue=DeclinedTransaction)for more details. | Hard |  |\n| [2012\n\n](#code-2012) | Processor Declined – Possible Lost Card | The card used has likely been reported as lost. The customer will need to contact their bank for more information. | Hard |  |\n| [2013\n\n](#code-2013) | Processor Declined – Possible Stolen Card | The card used has likely been reported as stolen. They will need to contact their bank or use a different payment method. | Hard | Visa: Category 1, do not retry |\n| [2016\n\n](#code-2016) | Duplicate Transaction | The submitted transaction appears to be a duplicate of a previously submitted transaction and was declined to prevent charging the same card twice for the same service. | Soft |  |\n| [2017\n\n](#code-2017) | Cardholder Stopped Billing | The customer requested a cancellation of a single transaction – reach out to them for more information. | Hard | Visa: Category 1, do not retry |\n| [2018\n\n](#code-2018) | Cardholder Stopped All Billing | The customer requested the cancellation of a recurring transaction or subscription – reach out to them for more information. | Hard | Visa: Category 1, do not retry |\n| [2019\n\n](#code-2019) | Invalid Transaction | The customer’s bank declined the transaction, typically because the card in question does not support this type of transaction – for example, the customer used an FSA debit card for a non-healthcare related purchase. They will need to contact their bank for more information. | Hard | Visa: Category 1, do not retry |\n| [2020\n\n](#code-2020) | Violation | The customer will need to contact their bank for more information. | Hard | Visa: Category 2, limit retries to 15 attempts over a rolling 30-day period |\n| [2021\n\n](#code-2021) | Security Violation | The customer's bank is declining the transaction, possibly due to a fraud concern.
